# ğŸš€ Ğ Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ³ Ğ¸ Ğ¡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¼Ğ° Ğ Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹

## ğŸ“ Layout Groups (Route Groups)

Next.js App Router Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµÑ‚ layout groups Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¿Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¼ Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ²Ğ»Ğ¸ÑĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğ° URL ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñƒ.

### Layout Group Architecture

```
app/
â”œâ”€â”€ layout.tsx              # âœ… Root Layout (Ğ²ÑĞµĞ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ²ĞµĞ½)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Navbar              # ğŸŒ Ğ“Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ Main Content        # ğŸ“„ ĞœĞµĞ½ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ² Ğ·Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸ÑĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ°
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Footer              # ğŸŒ Ğ“Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„ÑƒÑ‚ĞµÑ€
â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€ (auth)/                 # ğŸ‘¤ Route Group: ĞĞµĞ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ layout.tsx          # Auth Guard: Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½

â”œâ”€â”€ (user)/                 # ğŸ‘¥ Route Group: ĞÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ (USER+)
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ layout.tsx          # Auth Guard: Ñ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

â”‚

    â”œâ”€â”€ layout.tsx          # Role Guard: Ñ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ ADMIN+
    â”œâ”€â”€ loading.tsx         # Loading Ğ´Ğ»Ñ admin ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†
    â””â”€â”€ admin/page.tsx     # /admin
```

## ğŸ” Ğ¡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¼Ğ° Ğ Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹

### Ğ˜ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ Ğ Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹

```typescript
type UserRole = "USER" | "CREATOR" | "ADMIN" | "SUPER_ADMIN";

const roleHierarchy: Record<UserRole, number> = {
  USER: 1, // Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ
  CREATOR: 2, // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ° + USER Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°
  ADMIN: 3, // ĞĞ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€ + CREATOR + USER Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°
  SUPER_ADMIN: 4, // Ğ¡ÑƒĞ¿ĞµÑ€ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ + Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°
};
```

### ĞŸÑ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ° Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ°

| Ğ Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ            | Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹                                         | ĞĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ                       |
| --------------- | ------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| **ĞĞ½Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹**   | `/login`, `/auth/*`                                     | Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ |
| **USER**        | `/`, `/marketplace`, `/inventory`, `/docs`, `/settings` | Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ       |
| **CREATOR**     | USER + `/labs`                                          | Ğ­ĞºÑĞ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸      |
| **ADMIN**       | CREATOR + `/admin`                                      | ĞĞ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ»ÑŒ        |
| **SUPER_ADMIN** | ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿                                           | Ğ’ÑĞµ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ ÑĞ¸ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹            |

### ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ° (config/nav.ts)

```typescript
// ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ° Ğº Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¼Ñƒ ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñƒ
export function hasAccess(userRole: UserRole | null, item: NavItem): boolean {
  if (!userRole) return false;

  // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ (ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°)
  if (item.exactRole) {
    return item.exactRole.includes(userRole);
  }

  // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ (Ğ¸ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ°Ñ)
  if (item.minRole) {
    return roleHierarchy[userRole] >= roleHierarchy[item.minRole];
  }

  return true;
}

// ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
export function getAccessibleNavItems(userRole: UserRole | null): NavItem[] {
  return navigationConfig.filter((item) => hasAccess(userRole, item));
}
```

## ğŸ›¡ï¸ Auth Guards (Security Layers)

### 1. Middleware Guard (middleware.ts)

```typescript
// ĞŸĞµÑ€Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ ÑƒÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµĞ½ÑŒ - Ğ½Ğ° ÑƒÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ°
export async function middleware(req: NextRequest) {
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();

  // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
  if (!user && !isAuthRoute) {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/login", req.url));
  }

  // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ¿ĞµÑ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
  if (pathname.startsWith("/labs") && userRole === "USER") {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/", req.url));
  }

  if (
    pathname.startsWith("/admin") &&
    !(userRole === "ADMIN" || userRole === "SUPER_ADMIN")
  ) {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/", req.url));
  }
}
```

### 2. Layout Guards (Server-Side)

```typescript
// app/(user)/layout.tsx
export default async function UserLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  await requireAuth(); // Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
  return <>{children}</>;
}

// app/(creator)/layout.tsx
export default async function CreatorLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  await requireRole("CREATOR"); // Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ CREATOR+
  return <>{children}</>;
}

// app/(admin)/layout.tsx
export default async function AdminLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  await requireRole("ADMIN"); // Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ ADMIN+
  return <>{children}</>;
}
```

### 3. Server-Side Auth Utilities (lib/supabase/server.ts)

```typescript
// ĞšÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
export const getCurrentUser = cache(async (): Promise<User | null> => {
  const supabase = getServerSupabase();
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  return user;
});

// ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼
export async function requireAuth(): Promise<User> {
  const user = await getCurrentUser();
  if (!user) redirect("/login");
  return user;
}

// ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ Ñ Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼
export async function requireRole(
  requiredRole: UserRole | UserRole[]
): Promise<User> {
  const user = await requireAuth();
  const userData = await getCurrentUserData();

  if (!hasRequiredRole(userData.role, requiredRole)) {
    redirect("/");
  }

  return user;
}
```

## ğŸ¯ SPA Navigation (Single Page Application)

### ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ»ĞµĞ¼Ğ° Layout Re-rendering

**ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ»ĞµĞ¼Ğ°**: ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµÑ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ñ… Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ layout Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¿Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ğ²ÑÑ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¶Ğ°Ğ»Ğ°ÑÑŒ.

**Ğ ĞµÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ**: ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ½Ğ¾Ñ Navbar Ğ¸ Footer Ğ² root layout.

```typescript
// app/layout.tsx - Root Layout
export default async function RootLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <html>
      <body>
        <Providers>
          <SupabaseProvider>
            <ThemeProvider>
              <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-background">
                <Navbar />           {/* âœ… Ğ’ÑĞµĞ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ */}
                <main className="flex-1">
                  {children}         {/* ğŸ”„ ĞœĞµĞ½ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ² Ğ·Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸ÑĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ° */}
                </main>
                <Footer />           {/* âœ… Ğ’ÑĞµĞ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ */}
              </div>
            </ThemeProvider>
          </SupabaseProvider>
        </Providers>
      </body>
    </html>
  );
}
```

### Layout Group Simplification

```typescript
// app/(user)/layout.tsx - Ğ£Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ User Layout
export default async function UserLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  await requireAuth(); // Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

  return (
    <Suspense fallback={<UserLayoutSkeleton />}>
      <PageTransition>{children}</PageTransition>
    </Suspense>
  );
}
```

**Ğ ĞµĞ·ÑƒĞ»ÑŒÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚**: Navbar Ğ¸ Footer Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°ÑÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµÑ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ñ…, Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚ Ğ²Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸ main.

## ğŸ”„ Page Transitions

### PageTransition Component

```typescript
export const PageTransition = ({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) => {
  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: "easeOut" }}
    >
      {children}
    </motion.div>
  );
};
```

### Loading States

ĞšĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ°Ñ layout Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¿Ğ¿Ğ° Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞµÑ‚ ÑĞ²Ğ¾Ğ¹ loading.tsx:

```typescript
// app/(user)/loading.tsx
export default function UserLayoutSkeleton() {
  return (
    <div className="flex-1 p-6">
      <div className="container mx-auto space-y-6">
        <div className="h-8 w-64 bg-default-200 rounded animate-pulse" />
        <div className="grid gap-4">
          {[...Array(3)].map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-32 bg-default-100 rounded animate-pulse" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## ğŸª Route Examples

### Successful Flows

| URL            | Route Group | Required Role | Layout Chain                   |
| -------------- | ----------- | ------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `/`            | `(user)`    | USER+         | Root â†’ User â†’ Home Page        |
| `/marketplace` | `(user)`    | USER+         | Root â†’ User â†’ Marketplace Page |
| `/labs`        | `(creator)` | CREATOR+      | Root â†’ Creator â†’ Labs Page     |
| `/admin`       | `(admin)`   | ADMIN+        | Root â†’ Admin â†’ Admin Page      |
| `/login`       | `(auth)`    | None          | Root â†’ Auth â†’ Login Page       |

### Failed Flows (Redirects)

| URL      | User Role | Redirect To | Reason                 |
| -------- | --------- | ----------- | ---------------------- |
| `/`      | ĞĞ½Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ | `/login`    | Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ |
| `/labs`  | USER      | `/`         | ĞĞµĞ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²      |
| `/admin` | CREATOR   | `/`         | ĞĞµĞ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²      |
| `/login` | USER      | `/`         | Ğ£Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½        |

# ğŸ¨ UI/UX ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ‹

## ğŸ—ï¸ Layout Components

### Navbar (components/layout/Navbar.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚ Ñ role-based Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸ĞµĞ¹

```typescript
interface NavbarProps {}

export const Navbar = React.memo(() => {
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  const { supabase, session, role } = useSupabase() as SupabaseContextType;
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const [isMenuOpen, setIsMenuOpen] = React.useState(false);

  // ğŸ¯ ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ
  const navItems = useMemo(() => getAccessibleNavItems(role), [role]);
  const profileMenuItems = useMemo(
    () => getAccessibleProfileMenuItems(role),
    [role]
  );
  const isAuth = useMemo(
    () => pathname.startsWith("/login") || pathname.startsWith("/auth"),
    [pathname]
  );
});
```

**ĞÑĞ¾Ğ±ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸**:

- âœ… React.memo Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ re-render
- ğŸ”„ ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸
- ğŸ“± ĞĞ´Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ Ñ auto-close
- ğŸ¨ Ğ¦ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğ° Ğ´ĞµÑĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğµ
- ğŸ” Role-based Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²

**Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**:

```typescript
<HeroUINavbar>
  {/* Brand & Mobile toggle */}
  <NavbarBrand>
    <NavbarMenuToggle className="sm:hidden" />
    <NextLink href="/">MedTravel</NextLink>
  </NavbarBrand>

  {/* Desktop navigation - Ñ†ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ° */}
  <NavbarContent className="absolute left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 hidden sm:flex gap-6" justify="center">
    {navItems.map(item => <NavItem key={item.key} {...item} />)}
  </NavbarContent>

  {/* Right side actions */}
  <NavbarContent justify="end">
    <LanguageSwitcher />
    <ThemeSwitch />
    <ProfileDropdown />
  </NavbarContent>

  {/* Mobile menu */}
  <NavbarMenu>
    {navItems.map(item => <MobileNavItem key={item.key} {...item} onClose={() => setIsMenuOpen(false)} />)}
  </NavbarMenu>
</HeroUINavbar>
```

### Footer (components/layout/Footer.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: Ğ¡Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ñ„ÑƒÑ‚ĞµÑ€ Ñ ÑƒÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ñ€ĞµĞ½Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ¼

```typescript
export const Footer = React.memo(() => {
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  const { session } = useSupabase() as SupabaseContextType;
  const pathname = usePathname();

  // Ğ¡ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ„ÑƒÑ‚ĞµÑ€ Ğ½Ğ° auth ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°Ñ…
  const shouldHideFooter = useMemo(
    () => pathname.startsWith("/login") || pathname.startsWith("/auth"),
    [pathname]
  );

  if (shouldHideFooter) return null;
});
```

## ğŸ” Auth Components

### LoginManager (components/auth/LoginManager.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: State manager Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

```typescript
type AuthStep = "email" | "otp";

export const LoginManager = () => {
  const [step, setStep] = useState<AuthStep>("email");
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");

  return (
    <div>
      {step === "email" && (
        <EmailForm
          onSuccess={(email) => {
            setEmail(email);
            setStep("otp");
          }}
        />
      )}
      {step === "otp" && (
        <OtpForm
          email={email}
          onBack={() => setStep("email")}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

### EmailForm (components/auth/EmailForm.tsx)

**Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ**:

- ğŸ“§ Email OTP Ğ°ÑƒÑ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
- ğŸ” Google OAuth
- âœ… React Hook Form + Zod Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

```typescript
const emailSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email("auth.invalidEmail"),
});

export const EmailForm = ({ onSuccess }: Props) => {
  const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof emailSchema>>({
    resolver: zodResolver(emailSchema),
  });

  const handleEmailAuth = async (values: z.infer<typeof emailSchema>) => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({
      email: values.email,
      options: { shouldCreateUser: true },
    });

    if (!error) onSuccess(values.email);
  };

  const handleGoogleAuth = async () => {
    await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
      provider: "google",
      options: { redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/auth/callback` },
    });
  };
};
```

### OtpForm (components/auth/OtpForm.tsx)

**Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ**:

- ğŸ”¢ 6-Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ OTP ĞºĞ¾Ğ´
- â° Ğ¢Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ¼ĞµÑ€ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²ĞºĞ¸
- ğŸ”„ ĞĞ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ°Ñ Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ„Ğ¸ĞºĞ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

```typescript
export const OtpForm = ({ email, onBack }: Props) => {
  const [otp, setOtp] = useState("");
  const [timeLeft, setTimeLeft] = useState(60);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (otp.length === 6) {
      handleVerifyOtp(otp);
    }
  }, [otp]);

  const handleVerifyOtp = async (token: string) => {
    const { error } = await supabase.auth.verifyOtp({
      email,
      token,
      type: "email",
    });

    if (!error) {
      window.location.href = "/";
    }
  };
};
```

## ğŸ”„ Shared Components

### LanguageSwitcher (components/shared/LanguageSwitcher.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: Dropdown Ñ Ñ„Ğ»Ğ°Ğ³Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½

```typescript
const languages = [
  { code: "en", name: "English", flag: "ğŸ‡ºğŸ‡¸" },
  { code: "es", name: "EspaÃ±ol", flag: "ğŸ‡ªğŸ‡¸" },
  { code: "ru", name: "Ğ ÑƒÑÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹", flag: "ğŸ‡·ğŸ‡º" },
] as const;

export const LanguageSwitcher = React.memo(() => {
  const { i18n } = useTranslation();

  const currentLanguage = useMemo(
    () => languages.find(lang => lang.code === i18n.language) || languages[0],
    [i18n.language]
  );

  return (
    <Dropdown placement="bottom-end">
      <DropdownTrigger>
        <Button startContent={<Icon icon="solar:translation-linear" width={24} />} variant="ghost">
          <span className="hidden sm:inline">{currentLanguage.flag}</span>
        </Button>
      </DropdownTrigger>
      <DropdownMenu onSelectionChange={(keys) => {
        const selectedKey = Array.from(keys)[0] as string;
        if (selectedKey) i18n.changeLanguage(selectedKey);
      }}>
        {languages.map(language => (
          <DropdownItem key={language.code}>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span>{language.flag}</span>
              <span>{language.name}</span>
            </div>
          </DropdownItem>
        ))}
      </DropdownMenu>
    </Dropdown>
  );
});
```

### ThemeSwitch (components/shared/ThemeSwitch.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: Toggle Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ light/dark Ñ‚ĞµĞ¼Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸

```typescript
export const ThemeSwitch = React.memo(() => {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useTheme();

  const toggleTheme = useCallback(() => {
    setTheme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light");
  }, [theme, setTheme]);

  return (
    <Button
      isIconOnly
      aria-label="Toggle theme"
      variant="ghost"
      onPress={toggleTheme}
    >
      {theme === "light" ? (
        <Icon icon="solar:moon-linear" width={24} />
      ) : (
        <Icon icon="solar:sun-linear" width={24} />
      )}
    </Button>
  );
});
```

### PageTransition (components/shared/PageTransition.tsx)

**ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°**: Framer Motion Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸

```typescript
export const PageTransition = ({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) => {
  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: "easeOut" }}
      className="w-full"
    >
      {children}
    </motion.div>
  );
};
```

```typescript
const NavItem = React.memo(
  ({ item, active, t }: { item: any; active: boolean; t: any }) => (
    <NavbarItem isActive={active}>
      <NextLink
        prefetch
        className={`font-medium transition-colors ${

        }`}

      >
        {t(item.label)}
      </NextLink>
    </NavbarItem>
  )
);
```

**ProfileDropdown - ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ dropdown Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»Ñ**:

```typescript
const ProfileDropdown = React.memo(
  ({ session, role, supabase, t, profileMenuItems }: Props) => {
    const handleLogout = useCallback(async () => {
      await supabase.auth.signOut();
      window.location.href = "/login";
    }, [supabase]);

    return (
      <Dropdown placement="bottom-end">
        <DropdownTrigger>
          <Button>
            <Badge color="success" content="" placement="bottom-right" shape="circle">
              <Icon icon="solar:user-linear" width={24} />
            </Badge>
          </Button>
        </DropdownTrigger>
        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownItem key="profile" className="cursor-default">
            <p className="font-semibold">{t("navbar.signedInAs")}</p>
            <p className="text-default-500">{session?.user?.email}</p>
          </DropdownItem>
          <DropdownItem as={NextLink} href="/settings">
            {t("navbar.mySettings")}
          </DropdownItem>
          {(role === "ADMIN" || role === "SUPER_ADMIN") && (
            <DropdownItem as={NextLink} href="/admin">
              {t("navbar.adminPanel")}
            </DropdownItem>
          )}
          <DropdownItem
            key="logout"
            color="danger"
            startContent={<Icon icon="solar:logout-linear" width={16} />}
            onPress={handleLogout}
          >
            {t("navbar.logOut")}
          </DropdownItem>
        </DropdownMenu>
      </Dropdown>
    );
  }
);
```

## ğŸš€ Next.js 15 Optimizations

### Bundle Optimization (next.config.js)

```javascript
const nextConfig = {
  // Ğ­ĞºÑĞ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
  experimental: {
    optimizePackageImports: [
      "@heroui/react", // Tree-shaking UI ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
      "@iconify/react", // ĞĞ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ğ¾Ğº
      "react-i18next", // i18n Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
      "framer-motion", // ĞĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ tree-shaking
    ],
    ppr: false, // Partial Prerendering (ĞºĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ)
  },

  // Ğ’Ğ½ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°ĞºĞµÑ‚Ñ‹
  serverExternalPackages: ["@supabase/supabase-js"],

  // Compiler optimizations
  compiler: {
    removeConsole: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production", // Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ console.log Ğ² Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°ĞºÑˆĞµĞ½Ğµ
    reactRemoveProperties: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production", // Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ React dev ÑĞ²Ğ¾Ğ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ²
  },

  // Webpack Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
  webpack: (config, { isServer }) => {
    if (!isServer) {
      config.optimization.splitChunks = {
        chunks: "all",
        cacheGroups: {
          vendor: {
            test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/]/,
            name: "vendors",
            chunks: "all",
          },
          heroui: {
            test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/]@heroui[\\/]/,
            name: "heroui",
            chunks: "all",
            priority: 10, // Ğ’Ñ‹ÑĞ¾ĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµÑ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ UI Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞµĞºĞ¸
          },
          supabase: {
            test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/]@supabase[\\/]/,
            name: "supabase",
            chunks: "all",
            priority: 10,
          },
        },
      };
    }
    return config;
  },
};
```

## ğŸ”„ React Performance

### Memoization Strategy

**1. Component Memoization**

```typescript
// Navbar - Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ re-render Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ğ°
export const Navbar = React.memo(() => {
  // ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
  const navItems = useMemo(() => getAccessibleNavItems(role), [role]);
  const profileMenuItems = useMemo(
    () => getAccessibleProfileMenuItems(role),
    [role]
  );

  // ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ¸ auth ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†
  const isAuth = useMemo(
    () => pathname.startsWith("/login") || pathname.startsWith("/auth"),
    [pathname]
  );
});

// Footer - ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚
export const Footer = React.memo(() => {
  const shouldHideFooter = useMemo(
    () => pathname.startsWith("/login") || pathname.startsWith("/auth"),
    [pathname]
  );
});

// ThemeSwitch - Ğ¼ĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ
export const ThemeSwitch = React.memo(() => {
  const toggleTheme = useCallback(() => {
    setTheme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light");
  }, [theme, setTheme]);
});
```

**2. Context Optimization**

```typescript
// SupabaseProvider Ñ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸ĞµĞ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑÑ‚Ğ°
export function SupabaseProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [supabase] = useState(() => createClient());
  const [session, setSession] = useState<Session | null>(null);
  const [role, setRole] = useState<UserRole | null>(null);

  // ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑÑ‚Ğ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµĞ´Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ re-render
  const contextValue = useMemo(
    () => ({ supabase, session, role }),
    [supabase, session, role]
  );

  return (
    <SupabaseContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
      {children}
    </SupabaseContext.Provider>
  );
}
```

**3. Expensive Computations**

```typescript
// ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ… Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹ Ğ² Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
const getAccessibleNavItems = useMemo(() => {
  return (userRole: UserRole | null): NavItem[] => {
    return navigationConfig.filter((item) => hasAccess(userRole, item));
  };
}, []);

// ĞœĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ¸ Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸
const hasAccessMemo = useMemo(() => {
  return (userRole: UserRole | null, item: NavItem): boolean => {
    if (!userRole) return false;

    if (item.exactRole) {
      return item.exactRole.includes(userRole);
    }

    if (item.minRole) {
      return roleHierarchy[userRole] >= roleHierarchy[item.minRole];
    }

    return true;
  };
}, []);
```

## ğŸ—„ï¸ Caching Strategy

### Server-Side Caching

**1. React Cache Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Server Components**

```typescript
// lib/supabase/server.ts
import { cache } from "react";

// ĞšÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Supabase ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚
export const getServerSupabase = cache(() => {
  return createServerClient<Database>(
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL,
    env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll: async () => {
          const store = await cookies();
          return store.getAll().map(({ name, value }) => ({ name, value }));
        },
      },
    }
  );
});

// ĞšÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
export const getCurrentUser = cache(async (): Promise<User | null> => {
  const supabase = getServerSupabase();
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  return user;
});

// ĞšÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»Ñ
export const getUserProfile = cache(async (userId: string) => {
  const supabase = getServerSupabase();
  const { data } = await supabase
    .from("profiles")
    .select("*")
    .eq("id", userId)
    .maybeSingle();
  return data;
});
```

**2. Middleware Caching**

```typescript
// middleware.ts
const roleCache = new Map<string, { role: string; timestamp: number }>();
const CACHE_TTL = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚

export async function middleware(req: NextRequest) {
  if (user) {
    const cacheKey = user.id;
    const cached = roleCache.get(cacheKey);
    const now = Date.now();

    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° ĞºÑÑˆĞ° ÑĞ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ»Ğ°
    if (cached && now - cached.timestamp < CACHE_TTL) {
      userRole = cached.role;
    } else {
      // Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ‘Ğ” ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ½ĞµÑ‚ Ğ² ĞºÑÑˆĞµ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞµĞº ÑÑ€Ğ¾Ğº
      const { data } = await supabase
        .from("profiles")
        .select("role")
        .eq("id", user.id)
        .maybeSingle();

      userRole = data?.role ?? "USER";

      // ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ĞºÑÑˆĞ°
      if (userRole) {
        roleCache.set(cacheKey, { role: userRole, timestamp: now });
      }

      // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞºĞ° ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞµĞ¹ ĞºÑÑˆĞ°
      if (roleCache.size > 1000) {
        for (const [key, value] of roleCache.entries()) {
          if (now - value.timestamp > CACHE_TTL) {
            roleCache.delete(key);
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

```typescript
// i18n.ts
const resources = {
  en: { translation: en },

i18n.init({
  resources,
  fallbackLng: "en",
  detection: {
    order: ["localStorage", "navigator", "htmlTag"],
    caches: ["localStorage"], // ĞšÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ ÑĞ·Ñ‹ĞºĞ°
  },
});
```

```typescript
  subsets: ["latin", "cyrillic"],
  display: "swap", // Ğ‘Ñ‹ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° Ñ fallback
  variable: "--font-roboto",
  weight: ["300", "400", "500", "700"],
  preload: true, // ĞŸÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° ĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ñ… ÑˆÑ€Ğ¸Ñ„Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
```

## ğŸ–¼ï¸ Image Optimization

### Next.js Image Config

```javascript
// next.config.js
images: {
  formats: ['image/avif', 'image/webp'],          // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ‹
  deviceSizes: [640, 750, 828, 1080, 1200, 1920, 2048, 3840], // ĞĞ´Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¼ĞµÑ€Ñ‹
  imageSizes: [16, 32, 48, 64, 96, 128, 256, 384],            // Ğ˜ĞºĞ¾Ğ½ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¸ Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½ÑŒĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ

}
```

## ğŸŒ HTTP Optimizations

### Headers Configuration

```javascript
// next.config.js
async headers() {
  return [
    {
      source: '/(.*)',
      headers: [
        {
          key: 'X-Content-Type-Options',
          value: 'nosniff',              // MIME type Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°
        },
        {
          key: 'X-Frame-Options',
          value: 'DENY',                 // Clickjacking Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°
        },
        {
          key: 'X-XSS-Protection',
          value: '1; mode=block',        // XSS Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°
        },
        {
          key: 'Referrer-Policy',
          value: 'origin-when-cross-origin', // Referrer Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ°
        }
      ],
    },
    {
      source: '/static/(.*)',
      headers: [
        {
          key: 'Cache-Control',
          value: 'public, max-age=31536000, immutable', // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ€Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ ĞºÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸
        },
      ],
    },
    {
      source: '/_next/static/(.*)',
      headers: [
        {
          key: 'Cache-Control',
          value: 'public, max-age=31536000, immutable', // Next.js ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ°
        },
      ],
    },
  ];
}
```

## ğŸ“Š Performance Monitoring

```typescript
// app/layout.tsx
import { Analytics } from "@vercel/analytics/react";
import { SpeedInsights } from "@vercel/speed-insights/next";

export default function RootLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <html>
      <body>
        {children}
        <Analytics />      {/* ğŸ“Š ĞĞ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹ */}
        <SpeedInsights />  {/* âš¡ ĞœĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ */}
```

### Custom Performance Monitoring

```typescript
// ĞÑ‚ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¸ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ¸ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
export const withPerformanceTracking = <P extends object>(
  Component: React.ComponentType<P>,
  name: string
) => {
  return React.memo((props: P) => {
    useEffect(() => {
      const start = performance.now();

      return () => {
        const end = performance.now();
        console.log(`${name} render time: ${end - start}ms`);
      };
    }, []);

    return <Component {...props} />;
  });
};
```

```typescript
// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Suspense Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ½Ñ…Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²
```

## ğŸ¯ Performance Metrics

### Core Web Vitals Targets

- **LCP** (Largest Contentful Paint): < 2.5s
- **FID** (First Input Delay): < 100ms
- **CLS** (Cumulative Layout Shift): < 0.1
- **TTFB** (Time to First Byte): < 800ms

### Current Performance

- âœ… **First Load**: 341kB shared bundle
- âœ… **Page Loads**: ~154B per page
- âœ… **SSR**: Instant server rendering
- âœ… **Hydration**: Fast React hydration
- âœ… **Navigation**: SPA-like transitions Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ¸ layout

## ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Architecture

### Row Level Security (RLS)

```sql
-- ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹
CREATE POLICY "Users can view own profile" ON profiles
FOR SELECT USING (auth.uid() = id);

CREATE POLICY "Users can update own profile" ON profiles
FOR UPDATE USING (auth.uid() = id);

-- ĞĞ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ³ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´ĞµÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸
CREATE POLICY "Admins can view all profiles" ON profiles
FOR SELECT USING (
  EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM profiles
    WHERE id = auth.uid()
    AND role IN ('ADMIN', 'SUPER_ADMIN')
  )
);
```

### Authentication Flow

```typescript
// Supabase Auth Ñ Email OTP + Google OAuth
const authMethods = {
  emailOtp: {
    signIn: () =>
      supabase.auth.signInWithOtp({
        email,
        options: { shouldCreateUser: true },
      }),
    verify: () => supabase.auth.verifyOtp({ email, token, type: "email" }),
  },

  googleOAuth: {
    signIn: () =>
      supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
        provider: "google",
        options: {
          redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/auth/callback`,
          queryParams: { access_type: "offline", prompt: "consent" },
        },
      }),
  },
};
```

### Database Schema

```sql
-- ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğ¸ (Ñ€Ğ°ÑÑˆĞ¸Ñ€ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ auth.users)
CREATE TABLE profiles (
  id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) PRIMARY KEY,
  email TEXT NOT NULL,
  role TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USER' CHECK (role IN ('USER', 'CREATOR', 'ADMIN', 'SUPER_ADMIN')),
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ĞĞ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¾Ğµ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.handle_new_user()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
  INSERT INTO public.profiles (id, email, role)
  VALUES (NEW.id, NEW.email, 'USER');
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

CREATE TRIGGER on_auth_user_created
  AFTER INSERT ON auth.users
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION public.handle_new_user();
```

## ğŸŒ Ğ˜Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ (i18n)

### ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° i18n

```typescript
// ĞŸĞ¾Ğ´Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹Ğµ ÑĞ·Ñ‹ĞºĞ¸
const locales = ["en", "es", "ru"] as const;
type Locale = (typeof locales)[number];

// Ğ¡ĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ´ĞµÑ‚ĞµĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ·Ñ‹ĞºĞ°
export function detectLocale(acceptLanguage?: string): Locale {
  if (!acceptLanguage) return "en";

  const preferredLocales = acceptLanguage
    .split(",")
    .map((lang) => lang.split(";")[0].trim().toLowerCase());

  for (const preferred of preferredLocales) {
    if (locales.includes(preferred as Locale)) {
      return preferred as Locale;
    }

    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° ÑĞ·Ñ‹ĞºĞ° Ğ±ĞµĞ· ĞºĞ¾Ğ´Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ñ‹ (en-US -> en)
    const langCode = preferred.split("-")[0];
    if (locales.includes(langCode as Locale)) {
      return langCode as Locale;
    }
  }

  return "en";
}
```

### Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ²Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ²

### ĞšĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚ÑĞºĞ°Ñ i18n ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

```typescript
// i18n.ts
import i18n from "i18next";
import { initReactI18next } from "react-i18next";
import LanguageDetector from "i18next-browser-languagedetector";

const resources = {
  en: { translation: en },
  es: { translation: es },
  ru: { translation: ru },
};

i18n
  .use(LanguageDetector)
  .use(initReactI18next)
  .init({
    resources,
    fallbackLng: "en",
    interpolation: { escapeValue: false },
    detection: {
      order: ["localStorage", "navigator", "htmlTag"],
      caches: ["localStorage"],
    },
  });
```

### Theme Provider Implementation

```typescript
// components/ThemeProvider.tsx
"use client";

import { ThemeProvider as NextThemeProvider } from "next-themes";
import { ThemeProviderProps } from "next-themes/dist/types";

export function ThemeProvider({ children, ...props }: ThemeProviderProps) {
  return (
    <NextThemeProvider
      attribute="class"
      defaultTheme="system"
      enableSystem={true}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
    </NextThemeProvider>
  );
}
```
